***teken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teken.html>teken</a> (989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tēkan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taikną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tekenen.html>tekenen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têkenen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tēkanen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taiknijaną</i>.

***telekinese.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:telekinese.html>telekinese</a> (30231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:telekinese.html>Telekinese</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">телекинез</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">telekinez</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed during a media hype about supposed telekinesis in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dietersheim" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dietersheim">Dietersheim</a>, Germany, in 1920.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tēlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tilon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tilōną</i>.

***teleport.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teleport.html>teleport</a> (112380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">teleportation</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:teleport.html>teleport</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">teleports</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">teleporting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">teleported</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To travel, often instantaneously, from one point to another without physically crossing the distance between the two points.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1980</b>,  Douglas Adams,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:restaurant.html>Restaurant</a> at the End of the Universe</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I <b>teleported</b> home one night<br />With Ron and <a href = vnd.unilang:sid.html>Sid</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:meg.html>Meg</a>.<br />Ron stole Meggie's heart away<br />And I got <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To move (an object) in this fashion, as by telekinesis.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to travel from one point to another without physically crossing the distance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">beam</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">teleportation</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">unteleported</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:teleport.html>teleport</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">teleports</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">science fiction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:teleporter.html>teleporter</a>.</li>
<li>A satellite ground station.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  D. K. Sachdev,  <cite>Business Strategies For Satellite Systems</cite>, page 131:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>Teleports</b> provide access to multiple satellites and other media as well. Independently owned teleports may also provide competitive access to different satellite systems.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In 1655 <a href = vnd.unilang:ontdekte.html>ontdekte</a> Christiaan Huygens <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:telescoop.html>telescoop</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootste.html>grootste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maan.html>maan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saturnus.html>Saturnus</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***teleurstellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teleurstellen.html>teleurstellen</a> (5032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> luere <a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i>, more frequently found with other verbs such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">setten</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teleur.html>teleur</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teleurstellen.html>teleurstellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappoint
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:teleurgesteld.html>teleurgesteld</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You have really <b>disappointed</b> him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***telg.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:telg.html>telg</a> (40098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">telch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:telg.html>telg</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telguz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tellen.html>tellen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:tellen.html>tellen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taljaną</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to matter, to be of significance</li></ol>

***tempeh.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tempeh.html>tempeh</a> (87462)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Indonesian language">Indonesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:tempe.html>tempe</a></i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kawi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kawi language">Old Javanese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kaw">tumpi</i> (a food made from starch and <a href = vnd.unilang:tempeh.html>tempeh</a>), or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Indonesian language">Indonesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="id">tapai</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fermentation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Historia_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Historia-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tempeh.html>tempeh</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tempehs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An Indonesian food made from partially-cooked fermented soybeans, mixed with a fungus (<i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rhizopus_oligosporus" class="extiw" title="w:Rhizopus oligosporus">Rhizopus oligosporus</a></i>).
<ul><li><b>2015</b>, Labodalih Sembiring, translating <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eka_Kurniawan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eka Kurniawan">Eka Kurniawan</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> Tiger</i>, Verso 2015, p. 1:
<dl><dd>The leaves <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> of use only to the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tempeh.html>tempeh</a></b> factories, which collected them every night.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tempel.html>tempel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">templum</i>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tempel.html>tempel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">temple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ridder.html>ridder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tempel.html>Tempel</a></i> here refers to the Temple Mount in Jerusalem.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A Knight Templar, knightly member of the Templar order</li></ol>

<p>From the similarity with <a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a>, cheese; tenengt;<a href = vnd.unilang:toes.html>toes</a>

</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ten <a href = vnd.unilang:minste.html>minste</a></i>.

<ol><li>at least
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>Kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tenminste.html>tenminste</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:durft.html>durft</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Come on <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <b>at least</b>, if you dare.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<p>Confusion with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ten <a href = vnd.unilang:minste.html>minste</a></i>: <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the <i><a href = vnd.unilang:woordenlijst.html>Woordenlijst</a> Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>Taal</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://woordenlijst.org/zoek/?q=tenminste"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tenminste.html>tenminste</a></i></a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a different meaning than <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://woordenlijst.org/zoek/?q=ten+minste"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ten <a href = vnd.unilang:minste.html>minste</a></i></a>, although they are in origin the same. See also <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://woordenlijst.org/leidraad/6/10/"><a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>Andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betekenis.html>betekenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschreven.html>geschreven</a></a>.
